  New signature:
  generate_candidates(image, structured_goal, objects) -> list[dict]

  Logic:
  1. Find target object center from objects list (match
  structured_goal["target_object"]); fallback to image bottom-center if not
  found
  2. Compute goal pixel from structured_goal + objects (reference object center
  + offset for spatial/relative; quadrant for directional)
  3. NUM_STEPS = ceil(max(W, H) / STEP_SIZE)
  4. Fan ¬Ī90¬į around goal direction with per-step angular jitter
  5. Clamp all waypoints to 5px inside bounds
  6. Return full schema including points_original (same as points_scaled until
  coordinate scaling is added in Phase¬†10)

  main.py update:
  - Pass structured_goal and scene_objects to generate_candidates()

  Validation after Phase 4:
  - python main.py --random runs cleanly
  - candidates.png ‚ÄĒ trajectories start from the detected object, not image
  center
  - log.json ‚ÄĒ candidates have goal_type, target_object fields

  ---
  Ready to implement?

‚óŹ Found the bug. The red block is at (132, 75) ‚ÄĒ above the image center y=120.
  For "left", _compute_goal_pixel returns (0, 120) which is below and to the 
  left of the block, so goal_angle = arctan2(120-75, 0-132) points
  left-and-down, biasing T3/T4/T5 downward.

  The fix: for directional_motion, set the goal angle directly from the
  direction keyword ‚ÄĒ don't derive it from a goal pixel. The pixel approach only
  makes sense for spatial/relative goals where a reference object determines
  the direction.

‚óŹ T1 and T2 now end at x=5 and x=51 (left edge), T3 drifts down due to angular
  jitter but starts heading left. The trajectories are now correctly directed
  left from the red block's position.

  The fix: for directional_motion, use the direction keyword directly as a fixed
  angle (left = ŌÄ) instead of deriving it from a goal pixel, which was
  introducing a downward bias based on where the object sat relative to the
  image center.

> update spec.md to include complete goal interpretation. update spec.md to     
  include: Goal Completeness Validation                                         
                                                                                
  The Goal Interpreter Agent shall determine whether the user prompt contains   
  sufficient information to derive a unique target state and executable         
  trajectory.                                                                   
                                                                                
  The agent shall extract:                                                      
                                                                                
  target object                                                                 
  action                                                                        
  direction or spatial relation                                                 
  reference object (if applicable)                                              
  movement distance (if specified)                                              
  target position (if specified)                                                
                                                                                
  The agent shall classify the movement specification into one of the following 
  categories:                                                                   
                                                                                
  Explicitly Specified Movement                                                 
                                                                                
  The prompt explicitly provides the required movement distance or target       
  position.                                                                     
                                                                                
  Examples:                                                                     
                                                                                
  Move the red block 100 pixels left.                                           
  Move the cup 5 cm north.                                                      
  Move the block to x = 150.                                                    
  Image-Derivable Movement                                                      
                                                                                
  The movement distance can be derived from the image using a reference object  
  or target spatial relationship.                                               
                                                                                
  Examples:                                                                     
                                                                                
  Move the red block left of the blue block.                                    
  Move the cup east of the ball.                                                
  Move the bottle next to the laptop.                                           
  Underspecified Movement                                                       
                                                                                
  The prompt provides a movement direction but does not provide sufficient      
  information to determine the final target state.                              
                                                                                
  Examples:                                                                     
                                                                                
  Move the red block left.                                                      
  Move the cup forward.                                                         
  Move the bottle upward.                                                       
  Shift the laptop.                                                             
                                                                                
  In such cases the planner shall not generate a trajectory until additional    
  clarification is obtained from the user.                                      
                                                                                
  Goal Completeness Interrupt                                                   
                                                                                
  The Interrupt Agent shall support an additional interrupt category:           
                                                                                
  INSUFFICIENT_GOAL_SPECIFICATION                                               
                                                                                
  This interrupt shall be raised when:                                          
                                                                                
  movement distance is not specified                                            
  target position is not specified                                              
  target spatial relationship is not specified                                  
  movement magnitude cannot be derived from the image                           
                                                                                
  When this interrupt is raised, the system shall request clarification from    
  the user.                                                                     
                                                                                
  Example clarification prompt:                                                 
                                                                                
  "The requested movement direction is understood, however the final target     
  position cannot be uniquely determined. Please specify one of the following:  
                                                                                
  distance to move                                                              
  target coordinates                                                            
  reference object                                                              
                                                                                
  Examples:                                                                     
                                                                                
  Move red block 100 pixels left                                                
  Move red block left of blue block                                             
  Move red block to x = 150"                                                    
                                                                                
  Trajectory generation, VLM reasoning, and validation shall not proceed until  
  the ambiguity is resolved.

         +goal string.

         +ring or None.

      69 +    target_position = coord_m.group(0) if coord_m else None    
      70 +

         +ied"

         + reference_object:                                             
      82 +        return "image_derivable"

> pivot cadidate generator seem to be select very random trajectories which are 
  not valid. add constraint around trajecotry gnerator. update spec.md for      
  following: PIVOT Candidate Generation for Complete Goals                      
                                                                                
  Once the goal is complete, candidate trajectories shall be generated toward   
  the interpreted final target state.                                           
                                                                                
  For explicit distance:                                                        
                                                                                
  compute final target point using direction and distance                       
                                                                                
  For spatial relation:                                                         
                                                                                
  compute goal region relative to reference object                              
                                                                                
  For image-derived target region:                                              
                                                                                
  compute reachable free-space region                                           
                                                                                
  Generated trajectories shall satisfy:                                         
                                                                                
  start at target object center                                                 
  move toward the interpreted final target state                                
  remain inside image boundaries                                                
  avoid unnecessary random detours                                              
  contain enough points to cover the full required movement distance            
  keep all coordinates within image bounds                                      
  Boundary and Direction Validity                                               
                                                                                
  Generated candidate trajectories shall be validated before VLM reasoning.     
                                                                                
  Reject a trajectory if:                                                       
                                                                                
  any point lies outside the image boundary                                     
  initial movement is inconsistent with the interpreted goal                    
  final point does not satisfy the structured goal                              
  path contains unnecessary large random detours                                
  path cannot be evaluated safely                                               
                                                                                
  The VLM Reasoning Agent shall only receive candidates that pass basic         
  deterministic validation, except in debug mode where rejected candidates may  
  be visualized separately for analysis.

      283  **Supported goal types:** `directional_motion`, `spatial_relat
           ion`, `relative_motion`.
      284  
      285 -**Requirements:**                                             
      285 +#### 4.4.1 Target Point Computation                           
      286  
      287 -- start from target object center (from grounding output)     
      288 -- generate candidates directed toward the computed goal region
      289 -- scale path steps to image size: `NUM_STEPS = ceil(max(image_
          -width, image_height) / STEP_SIZE)`                            
      290 -- add per-trajectory angular jitter to produce curved paths

      287 +The generator shall compute a concrete goal pixel before gener

      289 +| `movement_specification` | `goal_type` | Target point comput
          +ation |                                                       
      290 +|---|---|---|                                                 
      291 +| `explicit` ‚ÄĒ distance given | `directional_motion` | `origin
          + + direction_unit * distance_pixels` |                        
      292 +| `explicit` ‚ÄĒ coordinates given | any | Use `target_position`
          + coordinates directly |                                       
      293 +| `image_derivable` | `spatial_relation` | Reference object ce
          +nter + relation offset |                                      
      294 +| `image_derivable` | `relative_motion` | Computed from relati
          +on direction and reference center |                           
      295  
      296 +`NUM_STEPS` is computed from the Euclidean distance between or
          +igin and target point:                                        
      297 +`NUM_STEPS = ceil(distance(origin, target) / STEP_SIZE) + 1`  
      298 +                                                              
      299 +This ensures all trajectories contain enough points to cover t
          +he full required movement distance rather than a fixed step co
          +unt.                                                          
      300 +                                                              
      301 +#### 4.4.2 Trajectory Generation Requirements                 
      302 +                                                              
      303 +- start at target object center (from grounding output)       
      304 +- direct all candidates toward the computed goal pixel        
      305 +- fan candidates within `¬ĪFAN_ANGLE` of the goal direction (de
          +fault `¬Ī20¬į` for explicit/image-derivable goals; `¬Ī45¬į` if goa
          +l pixel is approximate)                                       
      306 +- add small per-step angular jitter to produce natural curved 
          +paths (jitter std `‚Č§ 0.10 rad`)                               
      307 +- scale step size so the path reaches the goal point within `N
          +UM_STEPS`                                                     
      308 +- clamp all waypoints to 5px inside image bounds              
      309 +                                                              
      310 +#### 4.4.3 Trajectory Validation                              
      311 +                                                              
      312 +Each generated trajectory shall be validated before being pass
          +ed to VLM reasoning. A trajectory is **rejected** if any of th
          +e following conditions hold:                                  
      313 +                                                              
      314 +| Condition | Reason |                                        
      315 +|---|---|                                                     
      316 +| Any point lies outside image bounds | Out-of-bounds waypoint
          + |                                                            
      317 +| Initial movement direction deviates `> 90¬į` from goal direct
          +ion | Direction inconsistency |                               
      318 +| Final point is farther from goal pixel than start point | Tr
          +ajectory diverges from goal |                                 
      319 +| Path contains a single-step detour exceeding `3 √ó STEP_SIZE`
          + pixels | Excessive random detour |                           
      320 +| Fewer than 2 valid points | Path too short to evaluate |    
      321 +                                                              
      322 +Rejected trajectories are discarded and replaced by re-samplin
          +g until `NUM_CANDIDATES` valid trajectories are produced, up t
          +o a maximum of `MAX_RETRIES = NUM_CANDIDATES * 5` attempts.   
      323 +                                                              
      324 +In debug mode (`DEBUG_CANDIDATES = True` in config), rejected 
          +candidates are included in `log.json` under `"rejected_candida
          +tes"` for analysis but are not passed to VLM reasoning.       
      325 +

          +sing them to VLM reasoning.

       6 +def _serialise(obj):                                           
       7 +    """Recursively convert non-JSON-serialisable types."""     
       8 +    if isinstance(obj, tuple):                                 
       9 +        return [_serialise(i) for i in obj]                    
      10 +    if isinstance(obj, list):                                  
      11 +        return [_serialise(i) for i in obj]                    
      12 +    if isinstance(obj, dict):                                  
      13 +        return {k: _serialise(v) for k, v in obj.items()}      
      14 +    # numpy scalars / Python floats                            
      15 +    try:                                                       
      16 +        import numpy as np                                     
      17 +        if isinstance(obj, np.integer):                        
      18 +            return int(obj)                                    
      19 +        if isinstance(obj, np.floating):                       
      20 +            return float(obj)                                  
      21 +        if isinstance(obj, np.ndarray):                        
      22 +            return obj.tolist()                                
      23 +    except ImportError:                                        
      24 +        pass                                                   
      25 +    if isinstance(obj, float) and math.isinf(obj):             
      26 +        return None   # JSON does not support Infinity         
      27 +    return obj

      30 +def build_coordinate_scaling(image_shape, objects, best_traject
         +ory):                                                          
      31 +    """                                                        
      32 +    Build the coordinate scaling block for log.json per spec ¬ß4
         +.10.                                                           
      33 +                                                               
      34 +    In the current pipeline no internal resize is applied, so  
      35 +    processing_size == original_size and scale factors are 1.0.
      36 +    The block is included for forward compatibility.           
      37 +                                                               
      38 +    Args:                                                      
      39 +        image_shape:     (H, W[, C]) of the processing image   
      40 +        objects:         list of grounded objects (with bbox / 
         +center)                                                        
      41 +        best_trajectory: trajectory dict with points_scaled / p
         +oints_original                                                 
      42 +                                                               
      43 +    Returns dict with processing_size, original_size, scale_fac
         +tors,                                                          
      44 +    objects_scaled, objects_original, trajectory_scaled, trajec
         +tory_original.                                                 
      45 +    """                                                        
      46 +    h, w = image_shape[:2]                                     
      47 +                                                               
      48 +    # No resize in current pipeline ‚ÄĒ original == processing   
      49 +    processing_size = [w, h]                                   
      50 +    original_size   = [w, h]                                   
      51 +    sx, sy = 1.0, 1.0                                          
      52 +                                                               
      53 +    def _scale_objects(objs, fx, fy):                          
      54 +        result = []                                            
      55 +        for o in (objs or []):                                 
      56 +            bbox = o.get("bbox", [0, 0, 0, 0])                 
      57 +            cx, cy = o.get("center", [0, 0])                   
      58 +            result.append({                                    
      59 +                "name":       o.get("name"),                   
      60 +                "bbox":       [int(bbox[0]*fx), int(bbox[1]*fy)
         +,                                                              
      61 +                               int(bbox[2]*fx), int(bbox[3]*fy)
         +],                                                             
      62 +                "center":     [int(cx*fx), int(cy*fy)],        
      63 +                "confidence": o.get("confidence", 1.0),        
      64 +            })                                                 
      65 +        return result                                          
      66 +                                                               
      67 +    def _scale_points(points, fx, fy):                         
      68 +        return [[int(p[0]*fx), int(p[1]*fy)] for p in (points o
         +r [])]                                                         
      69 +                                                               
      70 +    pts_scaled   = best_trajectory.get("points_scaled", []) if 
         +best_trajectory else []                                        
      71 +    pts_original = best_trajectory.get("points_original", pts_s
         +caled)                                                         
      72 +                                                               
      73 +    return {                                                   
      74 +        "processing_size":    processing_size,                 
      75 +        "original_size":      original_size,                   
      76 +        "scale_factors":      {"x": sx, "y": sy},              
      77 +        "objects_scaled":     _scale_objects(objects, 1.0, 1.0)
         +,                                                              
      78 +        "objects_original":   _scale_objects(objects, sx, sy), 
      79 +        "trajectory_scaled":  _scale_points(pts_scaled,   1.0, 
         +1.0),                                                          
      80 +        "trajectory_original":_scale_points(pts_original, sx,  
         +sy),

> I want o add the scope of deployment. update spec.md for this architecture of 
  deployment: 19. Deployment and Continuous Improvement                         
                                                                                
  After implementation and initial evaluation are complete, the system shall    
  enter a deployment evaluation phase focused on identifying failure modes,     
  improving reliability, and preventing regressions.                            
                                                                                
  19.1 Deployment Dataset                                                       
                                                                                
  A deployment dataset shall be maintained separately from the development      
  dataset.                                                                      
                                                                                
  The deployment dataset shall contain:                                         
                                                                                
  unseen images                                                                 
  unseen prompts                                                                
  difficult edge cases                                                          
  ambiguous instructions                                                        
  cluttered scenes                                                              
  object grounding failures                                                     
  collision-prone scenarios                                                     
  boundary-condition scenarios                                                  
                                                                                
  Deployment cases shall represent realistic user interactions.                 
                                                                                
  19.2 Trace Collection                                                         
                                                                                
  Every deployment execution shall generate a trace record.                     
                                                                                
  The trace shall contain:                                                      
                                                                                
  input image                                                                   
  original prompt                                                               
  structured goal                                                               
  detected objects                                                              
  grounding results                                                             
  interrupt decisions                                                           
  candidate trajectories                                                        
  VLM reasoning output                                                          
  VLMPC validation output                                                       
  collision analysis                                                            
  clearance analysis                                                            
  final selected trajectory                                                     
  final outcome                                                                 
                                                                                
  Traces shall be stored under:                                                 
                                                                                
  deployment/traces/                                                            
                                                                                
  Each deployment run shall be stored separately and shall not overwrite        
  previous traces.                                                              
                                                                                
  19.3 Human Review                                                             
                                                                                
  A subset of deployment traces shall be reviewed manually.                     
                                                                                
  Human reviewers shall determine:                                              
                                                                                
  whether the interpreted goal is correct                                       
  whether object grounding is correct                                           
  whether interrupts were appropriate                                           
  whether the final trajectory satisfies the user intent                        
  whether safety constraints were respected                                     
                                                                                
  The review outcome shall be stored with the trace.                            
                                                                                
  19.4 Open Coding                                                              
                                                                                
  Deployment traces shall be analyzed using open coding.                        
                                                                                
  The reviewer shall identify and label observed failure modes.                 
                                                                                
  Example codes:                                                                
                                                                                
  wrong_object_detection                                                        
  missed_object_detection                                                       
  incorrect_goal_interpretation                                                 
  incorrect_spatial_relation                                                    
  missing_interrupt                                                             
  unnecessary_interrupt                                                         
  boundary_violation                                                            
  collision_violation                                                           
  trajectory_selection_error                                                    
  coordinate_scaling_error                                                      
  VLM_reasoning_error                                                           
                                                                                
  Multiple codes may be assigned to a single trace.                             
                                                                                
  19.5 Axial Coding                                                             
                                                                                
  Related open codes shall be grouped into higher-level categories.             
                                                                                
  Example:                                                                      
                                                                                
  Perception Errors                                                             
                                                                                
  wrong_object_detection                                                        
  missed_object_detection                                                       
                                                                                
  Reasoning Errors                                                              
                                                                                
  incorrect_goal_interpretation                                                 
  incorrect_spatial_relation                                                    
  VLM_reasoning_error                                                           
                                                                                
  Planning Errors                                                               
                                                                                
  trajectory_selection_error                                                    
  coordinate_scaling_error                                                      
                                                                                
  Safety Errors                                                                 
                                                                                
  collision_violation                                                           
  boundary_violation                                                            
                                                                                
  Interrupt Handling Errors                                                     
                                                                                
  missing_interrupt                                                             
  unnecessary_interrupt                                                         
                                                                                
  The objective is to identify the dominant sources of system failures.         
                                                                                
  19.6 Golden Dataset Creation                                                  
                                                                                
  High-value deployment cases shall be promoted into a Golden Dataset.          
                                                                                
  A case may be promoted when:                                                  
                                                                                
  it represents an important failure mode                                       
  it represents a previously fixed bug                                          
  it is a critical safety scenario                                              
  it is a representative benchmark example                                      
                                                                                
  The Golden Dataset shall be stored separately under:                          
                                                                                
  dataset/golden/                                                               
                                                                                
  Each golden case shall include:                                               
                                                                                
  image                                                                         
  prompt                                                                        
  expected structured goal                                                      
  expected interrupt behavior                                                   
  expected trajectory outcome                                                   
  expected validation outcome                                                   
  19.7 Regression Testing                                                       
                                                                                
  Before any future system update, the Golden Dataset shall be executed         
  automatically.                                                                
                                                                                
  The updated system shall be compared against the expected outputs.            
                                                                                
  The objective is to ensure that previously solved problems do not reappear.   
                                                                                
  Metrics to track include:                                                     
                                                                                
  goal interpretation accuracy                                                  
  object grounding accuracy                                                     
  interrupt accuracy                                                            
  collision avoidance rate                                                      
  boundary compliance rate                                                      
  trajectory success rate                                                       
  golden dataset pass rate                                                      
  19.8 Continuous Improvement Cycle                                             
                                                                                
  The deployment workflow shall follow the cycle:                               
                                                                                
  Deployment Data                                                               
  ‚Üí Trace Collection                                                            
  ‚Üí Human Review                                                                
  ‚Üí Open Coding                                                                 
  ‚Üí Axial Coding                                                                
  ‚Üí Golden Dataset Update                                                       
  ‚Üí Regression Testing                                                          
  ‚Üí System Improvement                                                          
                                                                                
  This cycle shall be repeated whenever new failure modes are discovered.       
                                                                                
  19.9 Deployment Reporting                                                     
                                                                                
  The system shall generate periodic deployment reports containing:             
                                                                                
  total deployment cases evaluated                                              
  failure rate                                                                  
  most common open codes                                                        
  most common axial categories                                                  
  golden dataset growth                                                         
  regression test results                                                       
  improvement trends over time                                                  
                                                                                
  These reports shall be used to guide future system improvements.              

  Read 1 file (ctrl+o to expand)

       950 +## 19. Deployment and Continuous Improvement                 
       951 +                                                             
       952 +After implementation and initial evaluation are complete, the
           + system shall enter a deployment evaluation phase focused on 
           +identifying failure modes, improving reliability, and prevent
           +ing regressions.                                             
       953 +                                                             
       954 +---                                                          
       955 +                                                             
       956 +### 19.1 Deployment Dataset                                  
       957 +                                                             
       958 +A deployment dataset shall be maintained separately from the 
           +development dataset under `dataset/deployment/`.             
       959 +                                                             
       960 +The deployment dataset shall contain:                        
       961 +                                                             
       962 +- unseen images                                              
       963 +- unseen prompts                                             
       964 +- difficult edge cases                                       
       965 +- ambiguous instructions                                     
       966 +- cluttered scenes                                           
       967 +- object grounding failures                                  
       968 +- collision-prone scenarios                                  
       969 +- boundary-condition scenarios                               
       970 +                                                             
       971 +Deployment cases shall represent realistic user interactions.
       972 +                                                             
       973 +---                                                          
       974 +                                                             
       975 +### 19.2 Trace Collection                                    
       976 +                                                             
       977 +Every deployment execution shall generate a trace record stor
           +ed under `deployment/traces/`. Each trace shall be stored in 
           +a separate timestamped file and shall not overwrite previous 
           +traces.                                                      
       978 +                                                             
       979 +**Trace schema:**                                            
       980 +                                                             
       981 +```json                                                      
       982 +{                                                            
       983 +  "trace_id":             "<timestamp>__<image>__<goal_slug>"
           +,                                                            
       984 +  "input_image":          "path/to/image",                   
       985 +  "original_prompt":      "move red block left of blue block"
           +,                                                            
       986 +  "structured_goal":      { "..." },                         
       987 +  "detected_objects":     [ "..." ],                         
       988 +  "grounding_results":    { "..." },                         
       989 +  "interrupt_decision":   { "interrupted": false } ,         
       990 +  "candidate_trajectories": [ "..." ],                       
       991 +  "vlm_reasoning":        "T2 moves toward goal without obsta
           +cles.",                                                      
       992 +  "vlmpc_validation":     { "..." },                         
       993 +  "collision_analysis":   { "..." },                         
       994 +  "clearance_analysis":   { "..." },                         
       995 +  "final_trajectory_id":  2,                                 
       996 +  "final_outcome":        "success"                          
       997 +}                                                            
       998 +```                                                          
       999 +                                                             
      1000 +---                                                          
      1001 +                                                             
      1002 +### 19.3 Human Review                                        
      1003 +                                                             
      1004 +A subset of deployment traces shall be reviewed manually. Hum
           +an reviewers shall determine:                                
      1005 +                                                             
      1006 +| Review dimension | Question |                              
      1007 +|---|---|                                                    
      1008 +| Goal interpretation | Is the interpreted structured goal co
           +rrect? |                                                     
      1009 +| Object grounding | Were target and reference objects correc
           +tly detected? |                                              
      1010 +| Interrupt handling | Were interrupts appropriate ‚ÄĒ neither 
           +missing nor unnecessary? |                                   
      1011 +| Trajectory intent | Does the final trajectory satisfy the u
           +ser's intent? |                                              
      1012 +| Safety | Were all safety constraints (collision, boundary) 
           +respected? |                                                 
      1013 +                                                             
      1014 +The review outcome shall be stored with the trace:           
      1015 +                                                             
      1016 +```json                                                      
      1017 +{                                                            
      1018 +  "review": {                                                
      1019 +    "reviewer":             "human",                         
      1020 +    "goal_correct":         true,                            
      1021 +    "grounding_correct":    true,                            
      1022 +    "interrupt_correct":    true,                            
      1023 +    "trajectory_correct":   false,                           
      1024 +    "safety_respected":     true,                            
      1025 +    "notes":                "trajectory ends short of referen
           +ce object"                                                   
      1026 +  }                                                          
      1027 +}                                                            
      1028 +```                                                          
      1029 +                                                             
      1030 +---                                                          
      1031 +                                                             
      1032 +### 19.4 Open Coding                                         
      1033 +                                                             
      1034 +Deployment traces shall be analyzed using open coding. The re
           +viewer shall identify and label observed failure modes. Multi
           +ple codes may be assigned to a single trace.                 
      1035 +                                                             
      1036 +**Open code vocabulary:**                                    
      1037 +                                                             
      1038 +| Code | Description |                                       
      1039 +|---|---|                                                    
      1040 +| `wrong_object_detection` | Wrong object identified as targe
           +t or reference |                                             
      1041 +| `missed_object_detection` | Target or reference object not 
           +detected |                                                   
      1042 +| `incorrect_goal_interpretation` | Structured goal does not 
           +match user intent |                                          
      1043 +| `incorrect_spatial_relation` | Spatial relation parsed or a
           +pplied incorrectly |                                         
      1044 +| `missing_interrupt` | Interrupt should have fired but did n
           +ot |                                                         
      1045 +| `unnecessary_interrupt` | Interrupt fired on a valid, execu
           +table goal |                                                 
      1046 +| `boundary_violation` | Trajectory exits or approaches image
           + boundary unsafely |                                         
      1047 +| `collision_violation` | Trajectory passes through an obstac
           +le |                                                         
      1048 +| `trajectory_selection_error` | Suboptimal trajectory select
           +ed as best |                                                 
      1049 +| `coordinate_scaling_error` | Scale-back produced incorrect 
           +original-resolution coordinates |                            
      1050 +| `VLM_reasoning_error` | VLM shortlisted an incorrect or uns
           +afe candidate |                                              
      1051 +                                                             
      1052 +---                                                          
      1053 +                                                             
      1054 +### 19.5 Axial Coding                                        
      1055 +                                                             
      1056 +Related open codes shall be grouped into higher-level failure
           + categories to identify dominant sources of system failures. 
      1057 +                                                             
      1058 +| Axial Category | Open Codes |                              
      1059 +|---|---|                                                    
      1060 +| **Perception Errors** | `wrong_object_detection`, `missed_o
           +bject_detection` |                                           
      1061 +| **Reasoning Errors** | `incorrect_goal_interpretation`, `in
           +correct_spatial_relation`, `VLM_reasoning_error` |           
      1062 +| **Planning Errors** | `trajectory_selection_error`, `coordi
           +nate_scaling_error` |                                        
      1063 +| **Safety Errors** | `collision_violation`, `boundary_violat
           +ion` |                                                       
      1064 +| **Interrupt Handling Errors** | `missing_interrupt`, `unnec
           +essary_interrupt` |                                          
      1065 +                                                             
      1066 +---                                                          
      1067 +                                                             
      1068 +### 19.6 Golden Dataset Creation                             
      1069 +                                                             
      1070 +High-value deployment cases shall be promoted into a Golden D
           +ataset stored under `dataset/golden/`.                       
      1071 +                                                             
      1072 +**Promotion criteria** ‚ÄĒ a case may be promoted when it repre
           +sents:                                                       
      1073 +                                                             
      1074 +- an important failure mode                                  
      1075 +- a previously fixed bug (regression anchor)                 
      1076 +- a critical safety scenario                                 
      1077 +- a representative benchmark example                         
      1078 +                                                             
      1079 +**Golden case schema:**                                      
      1080 +                                                             
      1081 +```json                                                      
      1082 +{                                                            
      1083 +  "case_id":                    "golden_001",                
      1084 +  "image":                      "dataset/golden/images/golden
           +_001.jpg",                                                   
      1085 +  "prompt":                     "move red block left of blue 
           +block",                                                      
      1086 +  "expected_structured_goal":   { "goal_type": "spatial_relat
           +ion", "..." },                                               
      1087 +  "expected_interrupt":         { "interrupted": false },    
      1088 +  "expected_trajectory_outcome":"success",                   
      1089 +  "expected_validation_outcome":"T2 selected, no collision", 
      1090 +  "promotion_reason":           "fixed trajectory divergence 
           +bug"                                                         
      1091 +}                                                            
      1092 +```                                                          
      1093 +                                                             
      1094 +---                                                          
      1095 +                                                             
      1096 +### 19.7 Regression Testing                                  
      1097 +                                                             
      1098 +Before any future system update, the Golden Dataset shall be 
           +executed automatically and compared against expected outputs.
      1099 +                                                             
      1100 +**Metrics tracked per regression run:**                      
      1101 +                                                             
      1102 +| Metric | Description |                                     
      1103 +|---|---|                                                    
      1104 +| `goal_interpretation_accuracy` | Fraction of cases with cor
           +rect structured goal |                                       
      1105 +| `object_grounding_accuracy` | Fraction of cases with correc
           +t target/reference detection |                               
      1106 +| `interrupt_accuracy` | Fraction of cases with correct inter
           +rupt decision |                                              
      1107 +| `collision_avoidance_rate` | Fraction of final trajectories
           + with no collision |                                         
      1108 +| `boundary_compliance_rate` | Fraction of trajectories withi
           +n image bounds |                                             
      1109 +| `trajectory_success_rate` | Fraction satisfying the intende
           +d goal |                                                     
      1110 +| `golden_pass_rate` | Overall fraction of golden cases passi
           +ng all checks |                                              
      1111 +                                                             
      1112 +A regression is flagged when `golden_pass_rate` drops below i
           +ts baseline value.                                           
      1113 +                                                             
      1114 +---                                                          
      1115 +                                                             
      1116 +### 19.8 Continuous Improvement Cycle                        
      1117 +                                                             
      1118 +The deployment workflow shall follow this cycle:             
      1119 +                                                             
      1120 +```                                                          
      1121 +Deployment Data                                              
      1122 +  ‚Üí Trace Collection         (¬ß19.2)                         
      1123 +  ‚Üí Human Review             (¬ß19.3)                         
      1124 +  ‚Üí Open Coding              (¬ß19.4)                         
      1125 +  ‚Üí Axial Coding             (¬ß19.5)                         
      1126 +  ‚Üí Golden Dataset Update    (¬ß19.6)                         
      1127 +  ‚Üí Regression Testing       (¬ß19.7)                         
      1128 +  ‚Üí System Improvement                                       
      1129 +  ‚Üí (repeat)                                                 
      1130 +```                                                          
      1131 +                                                             
      1132 +This cycle shall be repeated whenever new failure modes are d
           +iscovered.                                                   
      1133 +                                                             
      1134 +---                                                          
      1135 +                                                             
      1136 +### 19.9 Deployment Reporting                                
      1137 +                                                             
      1138 +The system shall generate periodic deployment reports contain
           +ing:                                                         
      1139 +                                                             
      1140 +- total deployment cases evaluated                           
      1141 +- failure rate (fraction with any open code assigned)        
      1142 +- most common open codes (top 5 by frequency)                
      1143 +- most common axial categories                               
      1144 +- golden dataset size and growth                             
      1145 +- regression test results (pass rate vs. baseline)           
      1146 +- improvement trends over successive reporting periods       
      1147 +                                                             
      1148 +Reports shall be stored under `deployment/reports/` and used 
           +to guide future system improvements.

‚óŹ Here is the complete Phase 13 execution plan, ordered by dependency:

  ---
  Phase 13 ‚ÄĒ Evaluation Tests

  Infrastructure first:
  - Create evaluation/ directory with __init__.py and tests/ subdirectory with
  __init__.py
  - Add pytest to requirements.txt
  - Create evaluation/tests/conftest.py ‚ÄĒ shared fixtures: load tabletop image,
  build synthetic objects list, build structured goals for each type

  ---
  Test files ‚ÄĒ order of implementation (simplest to most complex):

  Group 1 ‚ÄĒ Pure logic, no image needed (fast, no I/O):

  1. test_goal_interpreter.py ‚ÄĒ 10 cases:
    - directional / spatial / relative / unknown parsing (offline fallback)
    - movement_specification classification for each type
    - movement_distance extraction ("100 pixels left")
    - target_position extraction ("x=150")
  2. test_interrupt_agent.py ‚ÄĒ 8 cases:
    - all 7 interrupt codes fire correctly
    - INSUFFICIENT_GOAL_SPECIFICATION on underspecified goal
    - No interrupt on valid explicit and image_derivable goals

  Group 2 ‚ÄĒ Image-dependent component tests:

  3. test_object_grounding.py ‚ÄĒ uses data/images/img_01.png:
    - ground_scene() returns list with correct schema fields
    - All objects have name, bbox, center, confidence
    - Annotations path returns correct object count
  4. test_candidate_generation.py ‚ÄĒ uses data/images/img_01.png:
    - 5 candidates returned for each goal type
    - All points within image bounds
    - goal_pixel field present
    - points_scaled and points_original present
    - NUM_STEPS scales with distance to goal
    - Validation rejects out-of-bounds trajectories
  5. test_collision_checker.py ‚ÄĒ uses data/images/img_01.png:
    - Collision-free trajectory returns collision=False
    - Trajectory through obstacle returns collision=True, colliding_object
  populated
    - Target object excluded from obstacle set
    - collision_point populated on collision
  6. test_clearance_analyzer.py ‚ÄĒ uses data/images/img_01.png:
    - minimum_clearance > 0 for clear trajectory
    - minimum_clearance = 0 for trajectory touching bbox
    - closest_object name populated
  7. test_vlm_reasoning_agent.py ‚ÄĒ uses data/images/img_01.png:
    - Returns {"selected_candidates": [...], "reasoning": "..."}
    - All returned IDs are valid candidate IDs
    - Works with structured_goal and objects inputs
    - Fallback fires when USE_VLM=False
  8. test_coordinate_transform.py ‚ÄĒ uses data/images/img_01.png:
    - build_coordinate_scaling() returns all required fields
    - processing_size and original_size present
    - objects_scaled and objects_original have same object count
    - trajectory_scaled and trajectory_original same length
    - coordinate_scaling block present in log.json

  Group 3 ‚ÄĒ End-to-end:

  9. test_pipeline.py ‚ÄĒ uses data/images/img_01.png + img_02.png:
    - Full run produces all 5 output files
    - log.json contains all required top-level keys
    - Interrupt run halts cleanly, writes log.json with interrupt code
    - move red block 100 pixels left ‚Üí no interrupt, T* selected, 0% collision

  Group 4 ‚ÄĒ Deployment phase (¬ß19):

  10. test_trace_collection.py ‚ÄĒ stub for now (deployment infrastructure not
  built yet):
    - Verify deployment/traces/ directory created on run
    - Verify trace filename is unique and timestamped
    - Verify all ¬ß19.2 fields present
  11. test_regression.py ‚ÄĒ stub for now (golden dataset not populated yet):
    - Load dataset/golden/golden_cases.json ‚ÄĒ skip if not found
    - For each case: run pipeline, compare structured_goal and interrupt to
  expected
    - Report golden_pass_rate
  12. test_dataset_preparation.py ‚ÄĒ stub for now (Phase 12 not implemented):
    - Skip with pytest.skip until RefCOCOg dataset is prepared

  ---
  Validation gate:
  python -m pytest evaluation/tests/
  --ignore=evaluation/tests/test_dataset_preparation.py -v
  All 10 non-dataset tests pass before Phase 13 is considered complete.

  ---
  Notes:
  - Tests 10‚Äď12 are stubs that skip gracefully ‚ÄĒ they don't block the test run
  - test_trace_collection.py and test_regression.py will activate automatically
  once Phase 12 and deployment infrastructure are built
  - All tests use SEED=42 for deterministic results

  ‚ĒĒ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēī‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēī‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēė

  The VLM is estimating positions that are off by ~15‚Äď30px. This is expected ‚ÄĒ
  Claude vision approximates bounding boxes on small 320x240 synthetic images.
  There are two solutions:

  Option A ‚ÄĒ Use HSV grounding for tabletop images (immediate, accurate)
  When USE_VLM_FOR_GROUNDING=True but the image is a tabletop colored-block
  scene, fall back to HSV detection. Downside: only works for colored blocks,
  not generalized images.

  Option B ‚ÄĒ Pass image dimensions more explicitly in the VLM prompt (better)
  The current prompt says "The image is {w}x{h} pixels" but Claude may still
  round to grid coordinates. We can improve the prompt to ask for more precise
  bboxes relative to visible color regions.

  Option C ‚ÄĒ Use dataset annotations (already supported)
  When running with ground_scene(image, annotations=annotations), the
  dataset-provided bboxes are exact. This is the intended path for the
  generalized pipeline ‚ÄĒ VLM grounding is approximate by design.

  For the tabletop dataset specifically, the cleanest fix is Option A ‚ÄĒ add an
  HSV fallback path to grounder.py that activates when
  USE_VLM_FOR_GROUNDING=False. The data/generate_images.py images have known
  HSV-separable colors, so HSV gives pixel-accurate bboxes.

  Which approach do you want?

> update spec.md to include : ### Grounding Source Priority                     
                                                                                
  Object grounding shall use the most reliable available source.                
                                                                                
  Priority order:                                                               
                                                                                
  1. Dataset annotations, when available                                        
  2. Deterministic tabletop HSV grounding, for synthetic colored-block scenes   
  3. VLM grounding, for generalized images without annotations                  
  4. Interrupt, if no reliable grounding source is available                    
                                                                                
  For tabletop colored-block images, HSV grounding shall be preferred over VLM  
  grounding because block colors are separable and pixel-accurate bounding      
  boxes are required for trajectory start point, collision validation and       
  clearance computation.                                                        
                                                                                
  VLM grounding may still be used for generalized images, but its bounding      
  boxes shall be treated as approximate and logged with source="vlm".

       85 +_HSV_COLORS = {                                               
       86 +    "red square": [

          +,

      110 +_MIN_BLOCK_AREA = 100   # px¬≤ ‚ÄĒ ignore noise contours         
      111 +                                                              
      112 +                                                              
      113 +def ground_scene_hsv(image):                                  
      114 +    """                                                       
      115 +    Detect colored blocks via HSV segmentation.               
      116 +                                                              
      117 +    Returns list of grounded objects per ¬ß4.1.2 schema with so
          +urce="hsv",                                                   
      118 +    or empty list if no blocks are found (caller should try ne
          +xt priority).                                                 
      119 +    """                                                       
      120 +    h, w = image.shape[:2]                                    
      121 +    hsv = cv2.cvtColor(image, cv2.COLOR_BGR2HSV)              
      122 +                                                              
      123 +    objects = []                                              
      124 +    seen = set()                                              
      125 +                                                              
      126 +    for name, ranges in _HSV_COLORS.items():                  
      127 +        mask = np.zeros(hsv.shape[:2], dtype=np.uint8)        
      128 +        for lo, hi in ranges:                                 
      129 +            mask |= cv2.inRange(hsv, lo, hi)                  
      130 +                                                              
      131 +        contours, _ = cv2.findContours(mask, cv2.RETR_EXTERNAL
          +, cv2.CHAIN_APPROX_SIMPLE)                                    
      132 +        for cnt in contours:                                  
      133 +            if cv2.contourArea(cnt) < _MIN_BLOCK_AREA:        
      134 +                continue                                      
      135 +            x, y, bw, bh = cv2.boundingRect(cnt)              
      136 +            x1 = _clamp(x,      0, w - 1)                     
      137 +            y1 = _clamp(y,      0, h - 1)                     
      138 +            x2 = _clamp(x + bw, 0, w - 1)                     
      139 +            y2 = _clamp(y + bh, 0, h - 1)                     
      140 +            cx, cy = (x1 + x2) // 2, (y1 + y2) // 2           
      141 +            key = (cx // 5, cy // 5)                          
      142 +            if key not in seen:                               
      143 +                seen.add(key)                                 
      144 +                objects.append({                              
      145 +                    "name":       name,                       
      146 +                    "bbox":       [x1, y1, x2, y2],           
      147 +                    "center":     [cx, cy],                   
      148 +                    "confidence": 1.0,                        
      149 +                    "source":     "hsv",                      
      150 +                })                                            
      151 +                                                              
      152 +    if objects:                                               
      153 +        print(f"[Grounder] {len(objects)} object(s) detected v
          +ia HSV")                                                      
      154 +    return objects                                            
      155 +                                                              
      156 +                                                              
      157 +# ------------------------------------------------------------
          +---------------                                               
      158  # Phase 1: Scene grounding ‚ÄĒ primary entry point
      159  # ------------------------------------------------------------
           ---------------
      160

‚óŹ Here is the full Phase 12 execution plan:

  ---
  Phase 12 ‚ÄĒ Dataset Preparation (scripts/prepare_dataset.py)

  What needs to be built:

  1. Directory structure (created by the script)

  dataset/
    development/
      images/              ‚Üź downloaded JPGs
      annotations.json     ‚Üź list of case dicts per ¬ß7.3 schema
    deployment/
      images/
      annotations.json
    golden/
      images/
      golden_cases.json    ‚Üź golden case schema per ¬ß19.6

  2. scripts/prepare_dataset.py responsibilities

  1. Download RefCOCOg from Hugging Face (datasets library) ‚ÄĒ google/refcoco or
  refcocog
  2. Split into development / deployment ‚ÄĒ e.g. 80 development cases, 20
  deployment cases, sampled from the RefCOCOg validation set
  3. Save images ‚ÄĒ write each image to dataset/<split>/images/<case_id>.jpg
  4. Generate annotations.json per case:
    - case_id, image, source_dataset, target_expression, bbox
    - generated_prompts ‚ÄĒ 3 prompts per case (directional, spatial, relative)
    - interrupt_prompts ‚ÄĒ 3 interrupt prompts (missing object, ambiguous,
  uninterpretable)
  5. Create empty golden dataset ‚ÄĒ dataset/golden/golden_cases.json as []
  (promoted manually via ¬ß19.6)

  3. Prompt generation logic

  ‚ĒĆ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē¨‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēź
  ‚Ēā   Prompt type   ‚Ēā                       Template                        ‚Ēā
  ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§
  ‚Ēā Directional     ‚Ēā "move the {target_expression} left" / "right" / "up"  ‚Ēā
  ‚Ēā                 ‚Ēā / "down"                                              ‚Ēā
  ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§
  ‚Ēā Spatial         ‚Ēā "move the {target_expression} east of the             ‚Ēā
  ‚Ēā relation        ‚Ēā {other_object}"                                       ‚Ēā
  ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§
  ‚Ēā Relative motion ‚Ēā "move the {target_expression} away from the           ‚Ēā

  ‚Ēā Missing object  ‚Ēā Replace target with a plausible but absent object     ‚Ēā

  ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§
  ‚Ēā Ambiguous       ‚Ēā Use a vague reference like "the object" or "that      ‚Ēā
  ‚Ēā                 ‚Ēā thing"                                                ‚Ēā
  ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§
  ‚Ēā Uninterpretable ‚Ēā Use direction-free prompt like "move the cup          ‚Ēā
  ‚Ēā                 ‚Ēā somewhere"                                            ‚Ēā
  ‚ĒĒ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēī‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēė

       58 +def load_case(case_spec):                                     
       59 +    """                                                       
       60 +    Load a dataset case from annotations.json.                
       61 +    case_spec format: "path/to/annotations.json:case_id"      
       62 +    Returns (img_path, goal, annotations_list)                
       63 +    """                                                       
       64 +    if ":" not in case_spec:                                  
       65 +        print(f"ERROR: --case format must be 'annotations.json
          +:case_id'")                                                   
       66 +        sys.exit(1)                                           
       67 +    ann_path, case_id = case_spec.rsplit(":", 1)              
       68 +    if not os.path.exists(ann_path):                          
       69 +        print(f"ERROR: Annotations file not found: {ann_path}"
          +)                                                             
       70 +        sys.exit(1)                                           
       71 +    with open(ann_path) as f:                                 
       72 +        all_cases = json.load(f)                              
       73 +    case = next((c for c in all_cases if c["case_id"] == case_
          +id), None)                                                    
       74 +    if case is None:                                          
       75 +        print(f"ERROR: case_id '{case_id}' not found in {ann_p
          +ath}")                                                        
       76 +        sys.exit(1)                                           
       77 +    # Image path is relative to the annotations file's directo
          +ry                                                            
       78 +    ann_dir = os.path.dirname(ann_path)                       
       79 +    img_path = os.path.join(ann_dir, case["image"])           
       80 +    # Use first generated prompt as the goal                  
       81 +    goal = case["generated_prompts"][0] if case.get("generated
          +_prompts") else \                                             
       82 +           f"move the {case.get('target_expression', 'object')
          +} left"                                                       
       83 +    # Build annotation list for ground_scene (target object + 
          +bbox)                                                         
       84 +    annotations = []                                          
       85 +    if case.get("bbox"):                                      
       86 +        annotations.append({                                  
       87 +            "name": case.get("target_expression", "target"),  
       88 +            "bbox": case["bbox"],                             
       89 +        })                                                    
       90 +    return img_path, goal, annotations                        
       91 +
